\DoxyCodeLine{00565\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ 24\ byte\ string\ class\ (can\ be\ as\ small\ as\ 17\ for\ x64\ and\ 13\ for\ x86)\ that\ can\ hold\ strings\ with\ length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00566\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ of\ up\ to\ 23\ chars\ on\ the\ stack\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ the\ last\ byte\ of\ the\ buffer\ is\ used\ for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00567\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ -\/\ the\ highest\ bit\ -\/\ if\ "{}0"{}\ then\ it\ is\ small\ -\/\ otherwise\ its\ "{}1"{}\ (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00568\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ capacity\ left\ before\ going\ on\ the\ heap\ -\/\ using\ the\ lowest\ 5\ bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00569\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ 2\ bits\ are\ left\ unused\ -\/\ the\ second\ and\ third\ highest\ ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00570\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ if\ small\ -\/\ acts\ as\ a\ null\ terminator\ if\ strlen()\ is\ 23\ (24\ including\ the\ null\ terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00571\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ the\ "{}is\ small"{}\ bit\ remains\ "{}0"{}\ ("{}as\ well\ as\ the\ capacity\ left"{})\ so\ its\ OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00572\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Idea\ taken\ from\ this\ lecture\ about\ the\ string\ implementation\ of\ facebook/folly\ -\/\ fbstring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00573\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kPR8h4-\/qZdk}}
